Li Huchen, the commander of the First Anti-Smuggling Brigade stationed in Songjiang, received orders from his superiors to lead a team to cooperate with the Changshu County government's public security team and the naval and land police to suppress bandits in Liuhe, Hupu, Baimao Port, and other areas. Commander Li led his subordinates, including Captain Shi Fugeng of patrol boat No. 1 and Captain Pu Jinrong of patrol boat No. 2, as well as patrol boats Nos. 2, 3, and 4 of the First Company (totaling five vessels), equipped with machine guns and small cannons, set sail at 9 AM yesterday morning to the aforementioned locations to cooperate with the military and police in searching for and suppressing bandits, in order to eliminate banditry and protect shipping.

In the Courtroom

Evil Aunt Suddenly Faints 139

▲ Continued Trial of the Case of Strangling the Daughter-in-Law

▲ Deceased's Brother Also Attends Court

▲ Defendants Deny Conspiracy to Murder

After the sudden death of Li Zhang, the eldest daughter-in-law of Li Qingfu, a patrolman from 615 Gordon Road Police Station, due to rumors of murder, the Special District Local Court ordered an exhumation of the body. The findings determined strangulation. The police have formally charged Li Qingfu, his wife Li Chen, and his two sons Li Yulong and Li Kun with violating Article 282 of the Criminal Code. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Tingqi opened the court and ordered the four male and female defendants to be brought to court for interrogation. The police lawyer, Wang Yaotang, stated that the results of the prosecutor's examination revealed rope marks on the neck of the body, bloodstains on the head, and teeth that had fallen out, undoubtedly indicating strangulation. Li Qingfu, after the death of his daughter-in-law, had sent a letter to the deceased's mother, still claiming that she died from a "sha" ailment. This letter has been submitted to the police by the deceased's brother. He now presents the case, stating that during the initial interrogation the day before yesterday, Li Yulong and Li Kun both claimed that they had returned home from their work at the public bus company around 1:30 AM on the night of the 27th of last month. The police have sent detectives to investigate the company and have found that their statement was completely fabricated. Li Yulong had left the company at 4 PM that day, while Li Yulong had left the company at 11 PM. This point should be noted, he said. At this time, Chen, the wife of Li Qingfu, who was standing in the defendant's box, suddenly fell backward, her face turning pale, her eyes open and unmoving. Those who touched her felt that her hands were as cold as ice, and she did not respond when called. Judge Wu, seeing her condition, believed that she had a sudden illness and immediately ordered the bailiffs to help her out of the courtroom. He ordered the forensic doctor to examine her first, and the prison director was instructed to send her to Guangren Hospital for treatment. After the disturbance, the court continued to summon the witness, Mrs. Zhan Li, who testified that she was a neighbor of the Li family. On the night of the 27th of last month, at 11 PM, she still saw the deceased washing clothes by the tap at the door. Another witness, Mrs. Fang Chen, testified that she saw the deceased arguing with her mother-in-law at 7 or 8 PM that evening, and her mother-in-law slapped her face once. She went to mediate. Undertaker Wu Genfa testified that when he was dressing the deceased, he found blood seeping out of her neck, and there were also injuries on her fingers. Zhang Laiyun, the deceased's brother, arrived in court and stated that he received a letter from Li Qingfu on July 7 of the lunar calendar, stating that his sister had died of a sudden "sha" ailment. When he arrived in Shanghai, she had already been placed in a coffin. His sister had been married to Yulong for three years, and her mother-in-law usually treated her poorly. In April of last year, her mother-in-law's sister came to his house and talked about the strained relationship between the mother-in-law and daughter-in-law. Judge Wu then questioned the defendant, Li Yulong, who stated that he did not initially know how his wife had died. After the trial opened the day before yesterday, his mother told his father, who then told him, that his wife had hanged herself. Judge Wu, seeing that he was unwilling to confess how he had murdered his wife, instructed him, "Your parents, brothers, and you are all defendants in the same case. Your whole family is in custody. If you can confess who masterminded the murder and who did it, you can save your whole family from suffering." Yulong then stated, "I returned home at 1 AM that evening. After going upstairs, I saw my wife being helped by my mother to sit on the bed. I asked what had happened, and my mother said that my wife was suffering from 'sha.' I went out to find a doctor, but it was late at night and there was no one to be found. So, I went back home and saw my mother still sitting on the edge of the bed, while my wife was lying down. Then I went downstairs. I really don't know when my wife died, but there was definitely no strangulation." Li Kun confessed, "I returned home at 1 AM that night and saw my father cooling off at the door. I asked why I was so late, and I told him that I had been playing at the dog racing track, which led to my father scolding me. I then slept on a makeshift bed in the living room. I woke up at 4 AM, and my mother told me that my sister-in-law had died from 'sha.'" Questioning Li Qingfu, he consistently claimed that he did not know. The court ordered the defendants to be returned to custody, and the trial was adjourned to September 17.

Case of Accusation of Rape

Dancer Leaves Shanghai 140

▲ Leaving a Letter Expressing Apology

▲ Stating She Did Not Enter Defendant's Room That Night

▲ Polish Youth Benefited Not a Little

▲ Borrowing a Gun Also Has Someone to Testify

The Polish youth, Adam Szyszlo, was accused of rape by Li Guifen, a dancer from the Jue Lu Dance Hall. The General Patrol Station sent detectives to 9 1/2 Hankou Road, 4th floor, to arrest the youth and seize an unlicensed handgun found in his possession. He was brought to the Special District Local Court. Because the defendant denied the rape, the court ordered the plaintiff to be sent to a doctor for examination before further interrogation. Yesterday afternoon at 2 PM, Judge Zhou Hanting resumed the trial. The plaintiff, Li Guifen, was not present. According to the police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, the police had sent detectives to summon the plaintiff, but she no longer lived at the original address, making it impossible to summon her. The reason for her absence is unclear. The defendant believes that the plaintiff made a false accusation and now dares not appear in court. The plaintiff's husband was also not present. Judging from the doctor's written report of the examination of the plaintiff, there were only a few brief words regarding the circumstances of the alleged rape. As for the defendant's possession of a private handgun, he was in violation of the regulations prohibiting military firearms. Next, Western Detective Wilson reported that he had been unable to find the plaintiff. He then inquired with the manager of the dance hall, who said that Li Guifen and her husband, surnamed Chen, and a Russian had resigned on the 30th of last month. The Russian left a letter in Russian, saying that if the police or the court came to investigate, they could read the letter. The letter had the signatures of Li and her husband. Judge Zhou ordered Zhang to submit the letter as evidence and summoned a Russian translator to translate the meaning of the letter. The letter generally stated that the Polish man was drunk that night and had a slight argument with Li Guifen, but Li did not actually enter his room that night. Due to a minor suspicion, a lawsuit had unfortunately been filed, damaging their friendship. Li deeply apologized and therefore decided to leave Shanghai, so she would not be able to attend the next hearing. Afterwards, the police lawyer and the defendant's lawyer had a mutual argument. The court ordered the defendant to post bail and set the date for sentencing as the 10th of this month.

Chinese-Japanese Love Affair

Scene of Double Suicide 141

Chinese Overseer and Japanese Maid

▲ Maid Dies from Abortion

▲ Overseer Hangs Himself Out of Deep Love

Number 63 Shi Gao Ta Road in Zhabei is the residence of Kimura, the Japanese manager of the Ewo Cotton Mill. He employs Bian Sheng Shen, a 36-year-old Chinese man from Tianjin, as an overseer, and a Japanese maid, who is young and beautiful. There are many Japanese residents in the area, and she is considered the most beautiful of the maids. She and Bian got along very well. Later, Kimura returned to Japan, leaving only these two servants to guard the house, which led to a Chinese-Japanese love affair. Unexpectedly, the product of their love had already been conceived. Recently, her pregnancy became increasingly apparent, making it difficult to hide. Kimura then returned to Shanghai. The maid, fearing trouble, went to a hospital to have an abortion. Unfortunately, she died from the abortion at 6 PM the day before yesterday. When the news reached Bian Sheng Shen, he felt that he was responsible for her death. Out of love, he decided to commit suicide. At around 8 PM, he went out alone to a tree in the cemetery in the Jiehang area, where he hanged himself with a silk trouser belt. When he was discovered yesterday morning, the Japanese consulate police station and concession police station arrived at the scene to investigate. The Public Security Bureau's Fifth District Police Station then ordered Wang Jinfu, a local security guard from the 91st map, to report the case to the Local Court yesterday afternoon. Prosecutor Wu Shixin arrived at the scene and examined the body, finding that he was wearing a white summer cloth gown, white cloth shorts and pants, white socks, and white shoes, all white. He determined that the death was caused by hanging. The body was ordered to be collected by family members for burial.

Six Bandits Executed Yesterday 142

▲ The Bandits Only Asked for Food and Drink

▲ Showing No Fear of Death

The bandits Jia Kuizhong, Li Zhaozhen, Zhou Ziqing, Wang Maoyi, Zhang Yubiao, and Liu Guicai were apprehended by the Huishan Police Station. After repeated trials in court, they were found guilty and sentenced to death. The Special District Local Court had received instructions from higher authorities to execute the bandits according to law. Yesterday afternoon at 2 PM, the court informed the handling police station to bring Jia and the other six men from the Western Prison to the court. Judge Cheng Shangfeng took the stand, informed the bandits that they would be executed today, and asked if they had any last words. Upon hearing the announcement, the bandits remained calm, showing no fear and having no last words. They only requested to be given food, drink, and cigarettes. Judge Cheng immediately ordered the bailiffs to purchase the items. After the prisoners were taken to the waiting room, they smoked and drank to their fill before being escorted by the detectives to the cars for transportation to the execution grounds at the Jiangsu Second Prison in Caohejing. The Local Court appointed Prosecutor Zhao Zhigui as the execution supervisor. Zhao brought his secretary Zhang Guowei and inspector Xuan Zhiming, along with Police Chief Yang Deshan, Police Officer Chen Xihui, and twelve bailiffs, who travelled in cars to the execution grounds at the Caohejing Second Prison. The criminals were escorted and Zhao, along with Warden Dong Changmin, questioned them about their names, ages, and origins. The prosecutor asked what their occupation was, and they all replied that they were professional kidnappers. The official asked if they had any words for their families, and they replied that they had no words, but asked for some wine. Their attitude was extraordinarily calm, showing no fear and facing execution with generosity, truly unconcerned with the law. The prosecutor ordered the execution to be carried out. Police Chief Yang then directed the executioners Xue Bingzhang and Yin Daoxu to carry out the executions. The bodies were taken to the hall for collection, sealed, and awaiting identification by relatives.

Faint Whispers of Lament 143

▲ Scene of Youth Jumping into the River

▲ Long Rescue Attempt Ended in Failure

At 7:30 AM yesterday morning, a man jumped into the river from a pier on Beijing Road to commit suicide. As he entered the water, waves splashed, and faint whispers of lament were heard. A Chinese constable on the shore noticed it and, following the sound, saw the water surface rippling outside the pier, but the man did not resurface. He then assisted the boatmen in searching for him, but there was no trace. He returned to report to the police station and notified the water police station by telephone. Before the man committed suicide, he had been pacing back and forth on the pier. Passersby suspected that he was playing and did not pay attention, so his clothing and age are unknown.

Shanghai South Bus

Revision of Fares for Routes 1, 3, and 2 146

▲Approved for Trial Operation by the Public Utilities Bureau

Previously, due to rising gasoline prices, city buses were unable to maintain operations. With the approval of the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau, fares on all routes were increased by two cents per ticket. However, the Shanghai South Bus routes 1, 3, and 2, which run parallel to the trams, have seen a sharp decline in passengers since the fare increase. Overall, business has decreased significantly compared to before. In light of this, and considering that the fare increase was disproportionately high for the short distances of these two routes, the company has revised the fare prices for the two routes. Route 1 will start at four cents, with an increase of three cents per stop thereafter (except for the section from Laoximen to Dongjiadu, which will be seventeen cents, with a discretionary increase of one cent), for a total of thirty-two cents for the entire route. Route 3 will also start at four cents, with an increase of three cents per stop thereafter (except for the section from Laoximen to Xinkaihe, which will be seventeen cents), for a total of twenty-three cents for the entire route. It is reported that the proposal has been submitted to the Public Utilities Bureau for approval on a trial basis.

He Xiong, the leader of the detective team of the Fourth District Public Security Bureau in Zhabei, received a tip-off yesterday from informants stating that Jiang Dehe, a wanted criminal involved in the robbery of the Pudong Yanjiaqiao Tax Bureau (i.e., the Jiangsu Provincial Cotton Tax Bureau), was hiding near Guangzhao Road. On May 4th of this year, he and his accomplice Cao San from Taixing robbed the Pudong Tax Bureau. Cao used a gun to intimidate, and they stole a total of six hundred yuan in foreign currency. They divided the loot on the way, with Jiang receiving two hundred yuan and Cao receiving four hundred yuan because he had a handgun. Cao also gave Cao's cohabitant Chen Bulou ten yuan. Because Jiang confessed to the robbery and the distribution of the loot, the director, considering the case involved a robbery, ordered that Jiang be sent to the bureau and instructed the police detectives to arrest Cao San, who was still at large, for questioning.

A Quarrel Over Two Steamed Buns

Woman Angered and Commits Suicide by Poisoning 148

Chu Guocheng, a Ningbo native, forty years old, runs a carving workshop at No. 22 Youheng Road, Gongping Road, Hongkou. He married Tong many years ago. Tong is thirty-one years old. Their relationship was usually very close. They had been married for over ten years and had a daughter who had already passed away. Yesterday morning, Chu ordered an apprentice to buy dozens of steamed buns for the guest master's breakfast. At that time, a friend came to visit, and Chu was briefly occupied with him. Tong saw the many steamed buns on the table and took two to eat at will. After the friend left, Chu blamed Tong for grabbing the steamed buns in front of a guest, which was not proper for a woman. Tong refused to be outdone and retorted. Chu became angry and hit Tong several times with a wooden stick. Tong was extremely distressed and cried uncontrollably. By lunchtime, she refused to eat. Chu did not pay much attention to it at the time. Until after 3:00 PM, Tong instructed the apprentice to enter the room and call her fellow villager Luo Aru into the room. She said to Luo that when he returned to his hometown, please send a message to my mother, as I fear I will not be able to see her again. Luo saw that her face had changed dramatically, and she was moaning constantly. He suspected that she had taken poison and immediately reported it to the police. She was taken to Tongren Hospital in a vehicle. After the doctor tried to save her for a long time, it was ineffective. At around 5:00 PM, she was transferred to Guangren Hospital for treatment in an ambulance. As of 9:00 PM, she was still in critical condition.

Firearm Serial Number Doesn't Match Passport 149

Wang Yunde, a squad member of the Second Detachment of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau's Water Patrol Team, was patrolling the river yesterday near the new garbage bridge on the Suzhou Creek when he saw a boat speeding forward. He immediately ordered it to stop and then boarded the boat to conduct an inspection. He found 25 Mauser pistols hidden in a large wooden box in the cabin. He also found 12,500 rounds of ammunition in three small wooden boxes next to it. At that time, Wang Zhaozi and Chen Renliang, who were escorting the firearms, presented a passport issued by the National Government for verification. The squad member found that the number of firearms listed on the passport did not match the actual number being transported, suggesting suspected private smuggling. He detained Wang and Chen, along with Chen Baoan, the boatman, and the seized evidence, and brought them back to the detachment. During questioning by the patrol officer, Wang and Chen confessed that they were employees of the Asia Commercial Transport Company and that the firearms were arranged by their boss, Lin Wenguang, and Guo Yiting, who then sent them to hire Chen's boat to transport them to the Huitong Transport Company. They were then transferred to the South City General Team. Later, Asia sent another employee, Chen Junli, with a passport issued by the Director of the Aviation Department of the National Government, Zhang Huiliang, and a passport from the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining to the team, requesting the return of the seized firearms. Since the Aviation Department and the Lieshan Coal Mine Bureau were not related, and the passport from the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining had expired a month ago, there were many suspicions. They were ordered to prepare a document and submit it to the Third Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation and verification.

Why Must Grandmother, Granddaughter-in-Law, and Widow be Involved in Litigation? 150

An elderly local woman, Ni Jinshi, yesterday brought her widowed granddaughter-in-law, Zhao, to the Third District of the Public Security Bureau, claiming that she was sixty-six years old and lived in the Wu Family Alley behind the Lan Nidu Town in Pudong. Her husband died early, and she had maintained her chastity and raised her son for decades. However, the family's fortunes declined, and her son and daughter-in-law passed away one after another, causing the family's assets to dwindle. Now, only she and her granddaughter-in-law remain. After her grandson passed away in May of this year, her granddaughter-in-law became restless and moved elsewhere. She is now planning to sell the family property and remarry. Ni believes that remarriage is acceptable, but the property cannot be sold, leading to a family dispute. She came to the district to request a public judgment. According to Zhao, she is twenty-one years old, and after her husband died in May of this year, all expenses have been borrowed from outside. Now, she cannot pay the rent, so she plans to sell some of the household items to make a living. The District Chief, after reviewing the statements, considered that the pair of elderly and young widows were very pitiful. Was Yang Chongyu's Death a Suicide? 153

Yang Chongyu, a road policeman at the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway's South Station Police Department, had been repeatedly reported by the responsible patrol leader for dereliction of duty and had not reformed after admonishment. Police Chief Lou reported the situation to the two railway police headquarters for instructions, which ordered the dismissal of Yang Chongyu on September 1st. Unexpectedly, after his dismissal, Yang Chongyu suddenly sent a letter from Yong yesterday to Jian Huanluan, a patrol officer at the police department, claiming that he would commit suicide. The original letter is excerpted below: "Mr. Huanluan, I am leaving the station this time to seek my final peace, not because of my dismissal. It is only important to visit Poshen [referring to a temple], but my secret cannot be announced. I have been in adversity for more than a year, but my time in office was just a delay. What I am not satisfied with is that I could not settle my affairs before leaving, so I am writing to ask you to please give Zhang Yonggui one yuan from the three yuan of rice subsidy that will be issued later by my superiors, one yuan and some change to the snack shop behind the station, and ask Mr. Zhu Hongfei to take away the remaining boxes, mats, and luggage, which cost 2.11 yuan. I have already notified you separately about my own letter. Of the three yuan, there is still 0.09 yuan left, please give it to the person who washes my clothes, or give it to a guest who needs travel money, it's all the same. I ask you to please ask Shou Xinian and Chen Baochang to handle the above matters. Even in the disaster of being submerged, I know that they will be grateful. All colleagues, your opportunity to chat and laugh has arrived again. A smile, Yang Chongyu." It is found that Yang Chongyu was twenty-six years old, from Huai'an, Jiangsu, and was admitted to the two railway training schools in November of last year. On February 1st of this year, he was ordered to transfer to the First Platoon Police Department of the South Station.

Investigation into the Private Sale of Red Pills 158

The harm caused by red pills is worse than opium. The General Inspection Office received two confidential letters the other day. Chinese detectives Pang Ruiqing, Wu Hanzhang, Qiu Sijiu, and others, in cooperation with Western detectives, conducted an investigation based on the information in the letters. Zou Xueshi, a woman living in the back building, was found dividing red pills into small packages, each containing 18 pills, for sale at 20 cents per package. She was arrested, and three boxes of red pills were found on her person. Yang Xin'an, who lived in the front building, was found selling red pills to Tang Along for consumption. He was also arrested. Then, they went to No. 6 Hubei Road and arrested Zou Guoxiang, who was selling the pills. Zou was taking the pills at the time. Yesterday morning, they were taken to the Special District Local Court along with the seized red pills and the money earned from the sales. President Zhou Hanting interrogated them. Ru Baoyi, the police lawyer, stated that the harm caused by red pills was worse than opium, and that the defendants were engaged in this illegal activity and should be severely punished. President Zhou interrogated the defendants, who admitted to privately selling or consuming the pills without any disguise. Zhou sentenced Zou Xueshi and Yang Xin'an to one year in prison each, and fined them 360 yuan each. Zou Guoxiang was sentenced to one year in prison and fined 100 yuan. For the crime of private consumption, he was sentenced to two months in prison, to be served concurrently with the one-year sentence, and fined 100 yuan. Tang Along was sentenced to four months in prison and fined 40 yuan for privately consuming red pills. The red pills were confiscated.

The Social Affairs Bureau Establishes Factory Inspectors 163

▲ Promulgating Inspection Rules

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, in accordance with the Factory Law, should send personnel to inspect the factories and be responsible for guidance on whether the management and treatment of workers are good or not, and whether the workers are diligent or not. Therefore, it immediately drafted factory inspection rules to send personnel to inspect the factories at any time. These rules have been passed by the Bureau's 70th Bureau Affairs Meeting. They are recorded below. (Provisional Rules for Factory Inspection) Article 1. This Bureau is organizing factory inspections to improve the living conditions and work efficiency of workers in this city. Article 2. The time and location of the inspections will be determined by the director at any time and carried out by assigned personnel. Article 3. The duties of the inspectors are as follows: 1. To inspect the safety equipment, hygiene equipment, and working conditions of each factory, and provide appropriate guidance. 2. To investigate the difficulties in factory management. 3. To advise and supervise the implementation of relevant laws and regulations promulgated by the government. 4. To handle special assignments. Article 4. If the inspectors find that any of the following situations exist in any factory, they shall immediately report to the director for approval: 1. The workplace has poor air circulation, unclean drinking water, insufficient light, or no sanitary equipment. 2. There are no safety devices for the workers' bodies, factory buildings, and machinery installations. 3. Child and female workers are engaged in work that is harmful to public morals or has dangerous properties. 4. Workers do not obey management and guidance, which may hinder the factory's business operations. Article 5. Inspectors should take a peaceful attitude when inspecting. Article 6. Inspectors must report the results of each inspection to the director. Article 7. If the inspectors have any opinions on the improvement or crackdown of the inspected factories, they may submit them in writing to the director for adoption. Article 8. If the inspection requires the cooperation of other bureaus, this Bureau shall notify them at any time and send personnel to inspect together. Article 9. These rules may be amended at any time if there are any matters not covered. Article 10. These rules shall take effect from the date of approval by the director.

Negotiations on the Discharge of Chinese Employees by Citibank in Yokohama 164

▲ Should be Negotiated by the Minister to Japan with the Tokyo Branch

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce previously received letters from the Yokohama branch directly under the Chinese Kuomintang, requesting negotiations on the discharge of Chinese employees by the Yokohama and Tokyo branches of Citibank. The Chamber sent personnel to negotiate with the Shanghai branch of Citibank twice, but both times they were given empty words and evasions. After deliberation at a standing committee meeting, it was submitted to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for verification. A reply has now been received from the Social Affairs Bureau, which stated in summary that after sending personnel to investigate, Mr. Hogge, the manager of Citibank, claimed that the Shanghai branch was unaware of the discharge of Chinese employees by the Tokyo branch. Although the Shanghai branch is the Far East head office, the administrative power of the Tokyo branch is under the jurisdiction of the Far East branch of the New York head office. Therefore, this negotiation can be requested by the minister to Japan with the manager of the Tokyo branch. It is unknown why the Municipal Chamber of Commerce inquired about this matter in two letters, or perhaps it was a misunderstanding between the Far East head office and the Far East branch. Accordingly, since there is a misunderstanding about jurisdiction, the minister to Japan should be directly requested to order the subordinate authorities to negotiate directly with the Tokyo branch of the bank. If the negotiations are ineffective, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs should be requested to inform the U.S. Minister to the U.S., Wu, to negotiate with the Far East branch of the bank's New York head office. The Chamber will immediately forward a letter to the Yokohama branch for review.

Deadline for the Completion of the Coastal Radio Direction Finder 166

The Ministry of the Navy has ordered the Wusong Coastal Defense Command to set up a radio direction finder and to select sites at Jiuduan, Nanhui Mouth, and Putuoshan near the Wusong Estuary, so that ships can navigate the sea routes along the coast without errors in direction during fog and dew. Whether Promissory Notes are Exempt from Stamp Tax 167

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Shanghai Money Dealers' Association yesterday, stating that on the 4th of this month, it received a letter from the Hai'an Chamber of Commerce stating that the representatives of the Money Dealers' Association in the town inquired at the meeting, stating that each of the shops in their industry issues a type of promissory note (ranging from dozens to hundreds of yuan). This type of promissory note is issued by the shop in exchange for money brought by a person, making it easier to carry and having the same credit as cash, commonly known as "money tickets delivered to the door." It is similar in nature to bank checks. At present, the stamp tax inspection is strict. It is asked whether the promissory notes in their industry need to be affixed with stamps, and requested for instructions. A sample of the promissory note was attached. The Chamber has discussed the matter repeatedly and finds it difficult to make a decision. However, it recalls that in previous years, during the time of your former General Chamber of Commerce, there was a precedent for negotiating with the government to exempt bank checks from stamp tax. Since the promissory notes of the money dealers are equal in nature to checks, it seems that they can be exempted from stamp tax. However, the current laws and regulations are very strict, so it is not dared to be neglected. Therefore, a letter is sent with a sample of the note, requesting the Association to review and provide guidance on whether the aforementioned promissory notes can be exempted from stamp tax and whether the precedent for bank checks can be invoked. A detailed discussion and instructions are requested. It is also said that the money dealers in Shanghai also have a habit of using such promissory notes, and it is asked whether they are affixed with stamps, and for instructions. It is found that the stamp tax regulations, in the second category, have provisions for bank checks used by banks and money dealers, and notes of a similar nature, to be affixed with stamps according to the value. Therefore, the promissory notes seem to be within the scope of this provision. However, in the past, silver money dealers had submitted a request to the ministry to exempt checks from stamp tax. At present, it is not known whether the promissory notes can be exempted from stamp tax by invoking this precedent. Therefore, this letter is sent to request the Association to investigate and show the details, so that it can be passed along.

Stern Investigation into Impersonation by the Anti-Drug Association 168

Recently, the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association, based on a report from the Jianghai Customs, learned that someone was using the name of an official of the Association to report to the Customs about the private transportation of drugs, requesting a strict investigation. The Association is currently trying to investigate. Unexpectedly, someone else recently used the name of the Shanghai Municipal Anti-Drug Association to write a letter to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, accusing personnel there of embezzling drugs. All of these incidents have been investigated by the Anti-Drug Association. The Association believes that the matter of reporting is extremely important, and the Association had previously established and announced simple regulations for reporting documents. All matters such as reporting must be handled in accordance with the prescribed procedures to be appropriate and avoid abuses. Unexpectedly, cases of impersonation have been discovered one after another recently. If these are not investigated quickly, it will have a significant impact on the reputation of the Association. In addition to asking the government to strictly investigate the cases that have already been discovered, a notice is issued to all agencies and organizations as follows: (Respectfully, the Association has been handling external reports of disrupting the ban on opium and private transportation of drugs in accordance with the Association's regulations for reporting documents. After careful consideration, only when the evidence is deemed reliable will the Association forward the matter to administrative agencies for investigation in accordance with the law. This is to show seriousness and avoid abuses. However, it has recently been found that there have been repeated cases of impersonating the Association's name to act pretentiously, such as falsely using the name of an official of the Association to report the private transportation of drugs to the Jianghai Customs, and someone falsely using the name of the Shanghai Municipal Anti-Drug Association to report the embezzlement of seized drugs to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, requesting investigation. This is extremely shocking. If the above-mentioned incidents are true, they could be handled in accordance with the reporting procedures for forwarding to the relevant authorities for investigation. Why use a false name? It is obvious that there is another purpose. Fearing that the outside world does not understand the truth and will be misled, in addition to sending a letter to the local government to strictly investigate, we are hereby sending this special notice, hoping that you will take note of it. The future of the Association's work is of great importance. We wish you all the best, the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association.)

Jisheng Association Handles Disaster Relief in Yugou, Huaiyin 169

According to reports from Zhou Yuan-kai, Chairman, and Li Xilin, Vice-Chairman, of the Qingjiang Branch of the China Jisheng Association, Yugou in Huaiyin County is an important town in the county. On the 22nd of this month, it was attacked and breached by bandits, resulting in unspeakable acts of rape, looting, arson, and murder. Many victims have been displaced, without food or clothing, and are in urgent need of relief. Yesterday, Xu Jiaqing, the magistrate of Huaiyin County, telegraphed the Association and the Righteous Relief Association, requesting relief for the victims on behalf of the people. Kai and others are currently doing their best to raise funds, and plan to request permission to allocate some of the previously allocated flood relief funds to be used for emergency relief for the bandit disaster in Yugou, to save those in danger and prevent them from falling into ditches, etc. The Association has instructed the branch to carefully consider the situation, conduct a thorough investigation, and provide appropriate relief, so that funds are not wasted and the victims benefit. At the same time, the branch is urged to do its utmost to raise more funds to save the people from this great calamity.

Bandit Wang A'gen Sentenced to Five Years Imprisonment 172

Bandit Wang A'gen, together with a certain Jia (who has already been killed), each armed with a pistol, robbed Fang Lizhi, a native of Anhui, at 7 Lihe Lane, Beile Road, in the French Concession last month, obtaining 50 yuan. The bandits fled. One bandit fled north and was pursued by Annamese constables to Mahuo Road in the Public Concession, where he was shot dead. Wang fled east and was intercepted by Constable No. 206 at the intersection of Songshan Road. Two pistols and several silver dollars were found on the two bandits. The details of the case have been reported in the past. Yesterday morning, Wang was escorted to the French court for investigation. The plaintiff complained about the robbery at the time and claimed that the defendant was indeed the bandit who was holding a gun at the scene. He requested a severe punishment. Wang A'gen denied the charges, but the Chinese and Western judges ruled that the evidence was conclusive and there was no room for denial. Wang was sentenced to five years in the Western prison and then deported. The guns were confiscated and the stolen money was returned to the plaintiff.

British Soldier Boone Sentenced to Six Months Imprisonment 180

According to the Da Mei Evening News, Boone, a medical corps orderly of the British army, was charged with three counts: forging a letter of recommendation and a guarantee document from his superior, Ryder, and forging a promissory note to defraud an Indian of 250 yuan. After the preliminary hearing, he was tried at the British Military Court today (5th). British military authorities sent officer Baird to attend the trial. The defendant pleaded guilty, stating that he knew the matter was illegal and had sent a letter to the Indian after the fact, stating that the promissory note was false and that he would repay the money. He also said that he owed money to another British soldier, Maoli, who was an accomplice, so he forged the documents. The judge then sentenced him to six months imprisonment and hard labor. British soldier Maoli has been prosecuted in a separate case and was previously sentenced to one year imprisonment by the military court.

▲ Finder Please Deliver to the Police Station Quickly

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter 186

— Hai Ke

▲ Female Customer (going to a magazine office to ask a clerk) — I want to see the lady in your magazine who specializes in writing articles on women's issues. Is she in the office?

Clerk — She is standing over there talking to a friend. The one with the small mustache on her mouth and holding a thick cigar, that's her.

▲ Female Customer — Please show me your samples of oilcloth.

Shop Assistant — Yes, yes, yes. We have a lot of goods here. All sizes are available. Colors and patterns, all different. I don't know if madam wants to lay it in the living room or in the bedroom. What size do you need?

Female Customer — I want one to put in a birdcage. About one foot square is enough.

▲ Husband — I didn't come back last night. Who came to our bedroom?

Wife — No... no one else. But my sister came once.

Husband — This pipe and cane were forgotten here by her. Please return them to her. Then you should accompany your sister well.

▲ Art Buyer — An artist who is still alive, and a painting is priced at as much as three thousand yuan. Isn't that a bit too expensive?

Artist — Then how much money would you be willing to pay if I died? Please give me a number, and I will go die immediately.

Talking About an Old Diplomat 187

— Yu Yangzhou

Most of our country's diplomatic talents have lost power and territory. There are not many who can negotiate and protect the national interest. It is rare to find someone with a long-term vision who considers the world situation for far-reaching plans. I found Mr. Yao Ziliang among the predecessors.

Mr. Yao Ziliang is an old gentleman in Shanghai. Many people must know him. However, a piece of diplomatic history from his time in Europe may not be known to the people of our country. I am related to Mr. Yao. I heard about it from Mr. Yao himself. Mr. Yao traveled to Europe with Minister Hong Wenqing when he was young. Although Wenqing was the best in the country, he did not know the world situation. Mr. Yao studied economics and was also interested in geography and the art of diplomacy. At that time, Bismarck was the Prime Minister of Germany. The Franco-Prussian War had just ended. Germany leaped to become a strong country in Western Europe. Bismarck's vision had already penetrated the trend. The rise of the Germans would inevitably be envied by other countries and lead to a world war. The Germans' science and manufacturing were not to be feared, but the narrow land and dense population would inevitably feel insufficient in the production of raw materials. He wanted to unite a powerful and well-resourced ally to help him. At the right time, Mr. Yao met Bismarck in Berlin. Mr. Yao also believed that in a world where the weak are prey to the strong, it is necessary to form a strong neighbor as foreign aid. He talked with Bismarck about the affairs of the world. Heroes saw the same thing. Bismarck immediately proposed the opportunity for a Chinese alliance. His strategy was for Germany to provide manufacturing talents and set up factories in China to manufacture various weapons of war. Germany would provide capital, and China would provide raw materials. The products would be used for China and Germany to reorganize their military equipment. In the future, Germany would use its full strength to control the West to prevent French retaliation. China would control the East to provide mutual assistance. Mr. Yao believed that the Germans' move was sincere. The Germans wanted to control the whole of Europe and had no time to invade the East. This move was like using other people's strength, benefiting others and benefiting oneself, without malicious intent. He was very happy. He expressed concern that other countries would interfere. Bismarck also said that if international cooperation was inconvenient, the two countries could use commercial capital to sign contracts for commercial cooperation. The government would be the initiator behind the scenes, so there would be no problem. Mr. Yao was overjoyed and told the envoy. Mr. Hong thought that the matter was too important and did not dare to decide. He telegraphed the central government. At that time, Li Hongzhang was in power and did not dare to make a decision on his own. He reported the matter to the emperor. The Qing emperor also thought that the matter was too risky, so the discussion was shelved. Mr. Yao received the telegram and was unhappy for days. He told Bismarck about it. Bismarck also sighed in vain. In recent days, British and Japanese imperialism have been invading more and more. Our country is like meat on a cutting board, at the mercy of others. The Germans failed in the European War and were unable to recover. The reason for their failure was still the lack of raw materials. However, Duan was willing to declare war on Germany in alliance with the Entente Powers because of the loans for participating in the war. I would like to ask what achievements can be said to be achieved other than sacrificing tens of thousands of Chinese laborers and incurring debts of 30 million. Although Mr. Sun Yat-sen of the South strongly opposed it, it was ultimately ineffective. Therefore, we know how far-sighted Bismarck's vision was and how Mr. Ziliang's diplomatic skills compare to those of today's diplomats.

Recent News of a 253-Year-Old Man 188

— Chen Yuanliang

The news of the discovery of a 253-year-old man in Sichuan has spread far and wide. The Shanghai Pictorial even found a photo of him and published it in the newspaper. Many readers were also happy to see it.

However, because of the remote mountains and rivers, there has been no news about this old man for a long time. It is not known whether he is still alive. Recently, a certain lawyer from Sichuan who had just returned to Shanghai from his hometown gave a very detailed account of the old man's recent situation. It is written as follows for those who are concerned.

The lawyer's home is in Wanxian, and he recently returned to Sichuan to visit relatives. The old man lives in Kaizhou. The road is not far away. Because of an old family relationship, he was specially invited to his home and stayed for five days, eating and sleeping together. He observed his situation and asked about his secrets to longevity. According to him, the old man was from the middle years of the Kangxi period of the Qing Dynasty. He was from Guizhou. He came from a humble background. At the age of thirteen, he went out to collect medicine. He went into the deep mountains and out of the jungles. He had seen all kinds of tigers and leopards. He had been on the verge of death countless times. He had passed through Shaanxi, Gansu, Inner and Outer Mongolia, and Xinjiang. He had endured extreme cold and heat and suffered hardships. Later, he came to Kaizhou. Because of his old age and weakness, he settled there. He usually eats like a normal person. When he is hungry, he eats a lot. When he is not hungry, he often does not eat for several days. When he sleeps, he curls up like a bow. He sleeps lightly. Sometimes he does not sleep all night, and he sits upright in bed, like an old monk in meditation. Sometimes he is tired and sleeps, and the amount of sleep exceeds that of a normal person. However, when he sits, he must sit upright, without leaning or lying down. As the old saying goes, "sit like a bell." However, the old man's actions are extremely slow, like the stage steps of an old-fashioned drama civil official. His fingernails are very long and neatly arranged. It is very inconvenient to take things. Although the old man had little education in his youth, he was naturally intelligent and had a lot of experience. He is very clear about the warmth and dryness of medicinal properties, the cold and heat of the human body, and the changes in the climate. Patients ask him questions, and he can often cure them with one medicine. People are always grateful to him. He said that there is no secret to longevity, but he feels that he has always been open-minded, regardless of honor or disgrace. When he is hungry, he eats. When he is thirsty, he drinks. He treats people and handles things without harsh words or stern expressions. Today, people in Sichuan speculate that an old man of such a high age is rare in the world, let alone in China. He is a national treasure. This old man knows the properties of medicine, can cure diseases, and eats whatever is available and does not compete with the world. Therefore, he is beyond scientific civilization and enjoys a long life alone. Some say that the old man obtained a treasure that prolongs life when he was collecting medicine. Therefore, he has a floating and immortal state. Is that really the case? The lawyer initially planned to bring him to Shanghai, but the old man was not used to traveling by boat and car and disliked the noise of the sea. He declined and left.

Strange Tale of Being Struck by Lightning 189

— Lin Liqin

Yesterday, my maternal uncle came to Shanghai from his hometown. He spoke of a strange tale of being struck by lightning. Although it borders on superstition, it is enough to make the wicked and treacherous lose their chopsticks upon hearing it. Therefore, I do not hesitate to expend words to present it.

One day last month, the autumn heat was particularly severe. In the afternoon, dark clouds gathered. Soon after, heavy rain poured down, accompanied by thunder and lightning. At that time, in a certain village in Danyang, two or three farm women were bailing water from a river to irrigate their fields. Because the rain came suddenly, they did not have time to take shelter. Then, with a clap of thunder, it was said that all the farm women had been struck by lightning. Upon investigation afterward, it was found that only one person had actually been struck and killed. The other women had not been struck. They said that when the lightning suddenly struck, they were shocked and fainted. They only felt the smell of sulfur filling their nostrils. When they woke up and opened their eyes, they were crawling more than ten feet away. Only a certain woman was struck and killed, lying charred and stiff next to the waterwheel. The villagers found it strange. They all said that the women were in the same place, but the Thunder God only struck one person and, moreover, caused the surviving women to unknowingly move away from the spot. There must be a cause and effect. Several days later, the villagers again declared that the husband of the woman who was struck by lightning confessed his wife's sins to everyone. He said that his wife had long coveted the property of her younger brother. Her younger brother had been married for a long time but had no children. The wife thought that in the future, her son would inherit the property and continue the family line. Unexpectedly, last year, her brother's wife became pregnant and gave birth this spring. The wife pretended to help with the delivery but secretly devised a poisonous plan. When the newborn baby cried upon hitting the ground, she crushed its testicles. The newborn died instantly from the crushing. The wife pretended to be the spokesperson for her brother's wife, saying that the baby died as soon as it was born. The brother's wife believed it and only lamented her bad luck. Now, being struck by lightning must be divine retribution. Although these words are far-fetched, the speaker is earnest, and they come from her husband, so they may be credible. Therefore, those in the world who habitually use dark and evil tricks, upon reflecting on this matter, might they also know to be wary?

Film News 190

— Ping Yun

▲ A Record of Doctor Hồ's Melody: Since the advent of sound film, musical and dance films have become extremely popular. (Lili Damita) was one of the earliest releases, hailed as a leader in this genre. Bebe Daniels' name spread throughout the world as a result. The two comedic stars in the film, Wheeler and Woolsey, were also greatly praised by the world. The two were originally famous actors who played these two roles in Florenz Ziegfeld's stage play (Lili Damita). They have been doing this for three years, so they are familiar with it and feel more than competent. Recently, RKO Pictures, recognizing their popularity, urged them to take on the leading roles in the film "Cuckoos" (Doctor Hồ's Melody). Their comedy is even more outstanding than before, complemented by more than a dozen kinds of melodious songs and dances for embellishment, and dyed with natural color, extremely rich and resplendent. When it premiered in the United States, it caused a sensation across the country, and everyone praised it. It is now heard that this film has been acquired by the Dahua Hotel's open-air cinema and will be publicly screened tonight. The cool weather is not cold yet, so it's a great opportunity to entertain the eyes and ears. (Ping)

▲ A Record of Spiritual and Physical Conflict: The film Spiritual and Physical Conflict is produced by the German UFA company. The leading actors are the European actress Dida Barro, known for both her beauty and acting skills, and Lars Hanson, the male lead in (Flesh and the Devil) and (The Torrent). It depicts love and friendship. The plot is slightly similar to (Flesh and the Devil), but the acting is even better. The whole drama is full of moving romance and surprising tragedy. It is passionate and profound, unprecedented. It depicts the pain of longing in two places, enough to make emotional men and women shed tears of sympathy. And the final scene of returning home to face changes is especially impeccable. In short, the plot of this drama is quite suitable for the viewing habits of Easterners. It is said that when it premiered in a large theater in Japan recently, it was extended for three weeks, and the box office did not decline slightly. This can be seen in the success of the film. It is said that the film is currently being screened at the Paris Grand Theater. (Yun)

The Roman Catholic Church's Dissent Regarding Chinese Rites and Customs (Middle) 191

— Li Liuzeng, sent from Paris

However, at this time, Father Verbiest of the Jesuit sect in Beijing, due to his contributions to astronomy, regained his freedom and was appointed as the director of the astronomical observatory on April 1, 1669. Therefore, the Jesuit sect quickly regained its former power, while the Dominicans spread propaganda in Rome against France and the Jesuits. At that time, the Jansenists who surrounded King Louis XIV of France in Paris were also afraid that the success of the Jesuits in China would lead to their power infiltrating the French court, which would be detrimental to their future. Therefore, they vehemently attacked them. At that time, almost everyone who entered and exited the Palace of Versailles used Confucius and Chinese customs as topics of discussion. The great writer Saint-Simon also recorded this event in his "Memoirs." The gist of it was that the Jesuits recognized the worship of ancestors and Confucius by the Chinese as a kind of civilized custom, while other sects regarded it as superstition and idolatry, and argued incessantly.

The Jesuits in Beijing, knowing the seriousness of the situation regarding this issue in Rome and Paris, decided to express their opinions to the Qing Emperor Kangxi and Chinese ministers. On November 30, 1700, Emperor Kangxi declared the Jesuit interpretation to be correct. However, the Roman Catholic Church considered the testimony of the Chinese emperor who worshiped idols to be untrustworthy. Pope Clement XI issued an order on November 20, 1704, affirming that Chinese rites and customs were not civilized customs but a kind of superstition. However, this order was not made public but was only secretly delivered to the Papal Legate to China, Mgr de Tournon.

After countless twists and turns, on August 2, 1706, Emperor Kangxi summoned representatives of the two factions to the Rehe Imperial Villa, allowing them to debate the points of contention face to face. Subsequently, Emperor Kangxi personally arbitrated. Roughly speaking, one, the Chinese (Heaven) is the same as the Catholic (God). Two, the ritual of worshiping Confucius is not a kind of sacrifice (culte) but a kind of homage to a sage (hommage). Three, the meaning of worshiping ancestors is the same as the meaning of worshiping Confucius. Both of these do not conflict with the Catholic faith.

However, Emperor Kangxi's arbitration was as ineffective as the declaration of 1900. The dispute did not subside as a result. On January 25, 1707, Papal Legate de Tournon even read out a document in Nanjing refuting Emperor Kangxi's arbitration. Therefore, on April 1, Kangxi issued an edict prohibiting any missionary who did not accept the Jesuit interpretation of Chinese rites and customs from preaching in China.

Warmth in My Heart (270) 192

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 14: Green Bamboo Tears Stain Her Heart, Red Lotus Fragrance Fades as a Young Woman's Soul Departs

For the first month and a half, Cuiyun's business was very good. If she continued like that, she could gradually pay off her debts. Without debts, she would be even more free. As the saying goes, "Having a son makes everything complete, being debt-free makes life easy." In the brothel, just change one word, and it becomes "Having customers makes everything complete, being debt-free makes life easy." At that time, her father, Wu the silversmith, who had not been in contact for a long time, also came to recognize his daughter. Originally, Cuiyun had a lot of filial thoughts. Although she felt a bit of resentment towards her parents for being tricked into Shanghai by Sister A Xiu and being forced into a brothel, she thought that her old father was an honest man, and it was all her stepmother's doing. Moreover, she knew that Sister A Xiu was in cahoots with her stepmother. She still felt sorry for her father. In the past, it wasn't her own body, so there was no need to communicate with her father. Now that she could have a little autonomy, she asked someone to write a letter to her father, asking him to come to Shanghai to stay for a few days. Wu the silversmith couldn't have been happier to receive this letter. It was truly like "Hearing the invitation is like receiving a general's command." However, Cuiyun didn't mention her stepmother at all and didn't ask her to come to Shanghai with her father. That stepmother was still grumbling in front of the old man, saying that if it weren't for Sister A Xiu, how could she have today? She used to hate us, saying that we harmed her by making her eat brothel rice and ruining her life. Since that's the case, now that she's redeemed herself, she shouldn't eat brothel rice anymore. She should try to make a name for herself. Why does she still need to open a room? At this moment, she looked like she was serious. The old man ignored her, knowing that his daughter hadn't mentioned her in the letter. He secretly thought that his daughter still recognized him as her father. When he arrived in Shanghai, his daughter let him stay at her business place and treated him well every day. Knowing that her father liked to drink a little wine, she invited him to drink every day. Nothing is better than a cup in hand. After a drunken stupor, there were no problems. Because Cuiyun didn't have a small house, the old man had to sleep casually in the toilet at her business place. According to Cuiyun's intention, it was like preparing a sedan chair to welcome and support him. She didn't want him to go back to Kunshan again. However, Wu the silversmith, with his nature from the mountains and fields, couldn't get used to the extravagant atmosphere. He still wanted to retire and return to his hometown. Cuiyun made him several sets of clothes and also bought him many foods that were not readily available inland, such as assorted biscuits, for the old man to stave off hunger, and Cantonese sausages, for him to have with his wine. When Wu the silversmith returned to his township, everyone envied him. He had truly become a glorious homecoming. But he still didn't forget his affection for his wife and tried his best to mediate for Cuiyun's stepmother, saying that Sister A Xiu seduced you to go out in the first place, and your stepmother was also tricked. However, Sister A Xiu is hateful, but she owes her current status to her. He also whispered that your stepmother's lover died last year.

Grain: More Jiangxi Xian Arrives, Prices Rise Slightly 201

▲ Xiang Yuan Initially Opened at 320 Bags, Price 18.5 Yuan

Yesterday, another batch of Jiangxi rice arrived, and the market became even more depressed. Both the Northern Gang and inland areas had no appetite. Only the local streets, due to the high price of Du rice, found customer Xian rice to be more cost-effective, and their intentions were good. The total market transaction was 2,000 bags of early-season Jiangxi machine rice, priced at 13.85 yuan and 13 yuan, down to 12.6 yuan; 700 bags of late-season machine rice, priced at 15.8 yuan, 15 yuan, down to 14.23 yuan. Also, 80 bags of Hunan machine rice were sold at 13.5 yuan to 13.3 yuan. The Northern Gang's intentions were weak, and the Tianjin Gang was also watching and not moving. Yesterday, Xiang machine Yuan was dealt with at 320 bags, priced at 18.5 yuan, down to 17.8 yuan. Xiang Yuan rice grains are very large and have sufficient upward potential, so they are welcomed by local customers. This was the first time this batch of goods was sold, it is said.

Small Broken Rice Shipped Back from Hankou in Batches 202

Although the inventory of foreign rice is small, it is being squeezed by Jiangxi rice, and the market is quite weak. Transactions are also declining. The existing inventory in the market, except for Saigon No. 1, is all low-grade goods. Local streets have little appetite for low-grade goods. Only the Ningbo and Shaoxing gangs among the customer gangs may welcome it, but they are also being squeezed by Xiang and Gan rice. Yesterday, 300 bags of broken Da grain were sold at 11.95 yuan, down 4 to 5 fen from the previous day. Also, the small broken rice previously shipped to Hankou was difficult to sell due to the influx of Xiang rice in that area, and a batch was shipped back yesterday. The asking price was above 15 yuan, and no deal was reached due to disagreements with the shippers. However, the cost for that gang must be above 17 yuan.

Flour Market Suddenly Turns Downstream 203

Yesterday's flour market, after opening in the morning, both the current month and distant months were initially stable. However, after the second round, it gradually softened. This is because the quotation for foreign wheat has continued to decline by 2 to 3 jiao, and the pricing of foreign flour is indeed becoming cheaper. It is rumored that 3.95 yuan has already received a reply confirming the price, and 3.9 yuan is still under negotiation. As for the pricing of foreign wheat, Japanese merchants, taking advantage of the surplus tonnage on the Pacific, are offering discounts on shipping and touting No. 2 foreign wheat, opening at only 5.2 taels. Shanghai factories are countering with a price of 5 taels. Based on the current situation, this may become a reality. Because of this, each round in the afternoon was weaker than in the morning. Once foreign flour and wheat become cheap, even if those holding long positions want to resist further, they will feel overwhelmed. Therefore, the subsequent decline will depend on the pricing of foreign flour and wheat. As a result, the current month was down by 1 fen, October down by 2 fen, November down by 2 fen and 2.5 li, December down by 1.5 fen, and January down by 1 fen and 2.5 li, it is said.

Wheat Market Finds No Progress 204

▲ Foreign Wheat Reported Lower, Flour Sales Weak

Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat futures market in the morning, the various months were generally stable, with little change from the previous day's closing price. By the time the afternoon session opened, the market felt depressed due to the weakness of the flour market and rumors that the pricing of foreign wheat was about to be finalized. Market sentiment became even weaker, and buying interest was even more subdued. The various months also declined by 1 to 2 fen in light trading. If foreign wheat becomes cheaper and factories indeed cancel their orders, the price of wheat will naturally be affected. As a result, the current month was down by 1 fen compared to the previous day, October down by 1 fen, November down by 2 fen, December down by 1 fen, January down by 2 fen, and February was not opened. Currently, factories are still unwilling to budge, and the market is stagnant. Only 620 bags of inferior Shashi wheat were opened throughout the day at 4 taels 5 qian and 7 fen, and have not yet been allocated to factories, it is said.

Sugar Market: Rising Trend of Japanese Sugar Slightly Weakens 205

Yesterday's sugar market saw telegrams from producing areas reporting that the price of Cuban spot sugar was 1.15625, a slight decrease of 0.0625 compared to the previous telegram. The price of New York sugar futures for September remained at 1.12, December at 1.19, down 2 points, March of next year at 1.39, and May at 1.39, also down 1 point each. The price of Javanese spot sugar was 8.875, futures sugar for September at 8.8125, October at 8.625, November at 8.50, with only a slight increase of 0.0625 for the current month compared to the previous telegram, and no changes for the remaining months. In the public market, the buying interest in Dutch sugar No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar was sluggish, and transactions were few and far between. Ordinary goods were priced at 8 taels, and slightly higher ones at 8 taels and 1 qian. The market was flat and unremarkable. The Japanese sugar market also turned stable. This is because shipments continued to arrive, and after the previous surge in white sugar prices in various places, many were taking a wait-and-see approach. However, the Dali Factory market did not sell on return telegrams, so the market was still able to stand. S.H. brand opened at 8 taels to the price of 8 taels, and later at 8 taels 1 qian and 2.5 fen. N brand initially opened at 8 taels and 0.05 fen, YT brand at 8 taels and 0.075 fen, YP brand at 8 taels 1 qian and 7.5 fen, and J brand at 8 taels 2 qian and 7.5 fen. Transactions were not smooth, and the market appeared to have fallen back by 2.5 fen compared to the previous day. The trademark numbers Zhenxiang and Jinfeng opened spot coarse granulated white sugar at more than 2,000 bags, priced at 8 taels each. Because the total amount was nearly 20,000 bags, and the bank's intention to buy was very weak, it was not easy to sell them all at once, it is said.

Dried Goods: Longkou Vermicelli Rises Another 5 Qian 206

▲ Two Batches of Newly Dried Meat Arrive

▲ Longkou Vermicelli Due to the scarcity of goods in the previous market, the price once opened at 19.5 taels. However, the source of supply has remained lacking in recent days, so the trend has tightened again. Yesterday, it was reported that another batch of customer goods opened, with the price rising to 20 taels. Therefore, the selling prices of various firms have uniformly increased accordingly. Furthermore, the movement of various gangs has been lively in recent days, and the market is feared to tighten further.

▲ Newly Dried Round Meat The first batch has already been sold. Yesterday, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Dachang Wheel arrived in Shanghai from Xiamen, bringing a second batch of more than 20 pieces in total. If the goods are of high quality, the market price should not fluctuate excessively, it is said.

Piece Goods: Customer Sales Active, Prices Frequently Rise 207

The piece goods market situation continued to trend upwards yesterday. The liveliness of the cotton cloth market is unprecedented this year. Yoshida & Co. opened more than 300 pieces of Yuehua velvet, colored stripes, fine whipcord, etc., all with yesterday's cash settlement. The good market sentiment was rare. Large-pattern Yuehua velvet opened at 1 qian 9 fen and 5 li, medium-pattern Yuehua velvet at 1 qian 9 fen and 2.5 li, and small-pattern at 1 qian 8 fen and 5 li. Thick French velvet rose by 5 li yesterday. Dharma Lion concubine color at 2 qian 6 fen, white at 2 qian 5 fen. Those holding fine whipcord were hoarding and refusing to sell. Fellow traders were very eager to buy. It is said that although the price has risen by more than 1 fen in the past three days, it is still about 1 fen cheaper than tribute cloth and satin from the lower classes. Therefore, there is a unanimous expectation of further price increases. The Sichuan gang, which sells for actual use, also shows signs of activity. Yesterday, they telegraphed to buy more than 100 pieces. The Tianjin, Qingdao, Xuzhou, and Ningbo gangs were also quite active. Inland wholesalers are also very busy due to the arrival of the autumn season, and the price of goods shows a strong upward trend, it is said.

Hardware: East White Iron Sells Briskly 208

The East White Iron trade has seen increased transactions among customer gangs in recent days, so the volume being opened is quite considerable. Therefore, the market has also turned from weak to strong. It is estimated that each 36-inch sheet is worth 9 qian and 4 fen, and each 37-inch sheet is worth 1 tael 1 qian and 3 fen. It is reported that 2,500 to 2,600 sheets were opened yesterday, it is said.

Organization News 233

▲Pan Xulun Accounting Institute declares that since the establishment of the school, the achievements have been remarkable. This year's freshmen have more than 130 people. On the 7th of this month (Sunday) at 9:00 am, the opening ceremony will be held in the auditorium of the Sichuan Road YMCA. Mr. Jiang Wenyu, president of the Chinese Vocational Education Society, and Mr. Pan Yangyao, director of the Chinese Vocational Guidance Center, will give speeches on vocational issues. The school welcomes people from all walks of life to come and listen at that time.

Business News 234

▲Sincere Company declares that the foreign goods department of the store has newly arrived various styles of felt hats, with a complete range and satisfactory choices. The new style of Stedson's 30-year edition has also been displayed. The lowest price of felt hats is one yuan and eight cents per hat. In addition, women's handbags are sold at cost, and buyers have been extremely crowded in recent days. Women's long silk stockings are sold for one yuan per two pairs, various hair growth perfumes start from 45 cents per bottle, Western-style detachable collars are one yuan per half dozen, Western-style ties are brightly colored and sold for one yuan per three, and shirts are one yuan each.

▲Hanli Company declares that the Zhongling air pressure press is a new invention of domestic goods, simple and clear, and is the center of today's printing industry. The manager has traveled all over the country, and many foreigners are happy to use it. Recently, Mr. Luo Qincheng, a Siamese merchant, learned that the machine is suitable for printing both Chinese and Western characters. He came to Shanghai and reached an agreement with Hanli Company to transport a large number of printing machines back to Siam for sale. It is heard that Mr. Luo is an old friend of Mr. Zhongling, a classmate from Lingnan, and they are very close. Recently, he has been contracting to build railways in 14 provinces of Siam, with strong capital, the most influential, and a high reputation. Selling the machine through him will surely achieve success.

▲Lianmei Store at the intersection of Fada Road and Dongxin Bridge Street declares that it has been established for more than ten years and has a well-established reputation. Due to insufficient housing, a new three-story Western-style building has been built, with luxurious decorations, and has now been completed. During the opening period, Chinese and foreign merchandise are sold at discounted prices, and gifts are provided.

▲Fuxin Tobacco Factory declares that the factory was organized by Wang Junkang and others, and has been in operation for five years. All products have been praised by all sectors of society. Recently, a new type of red and green brand cigarettes has been launched, with golden silk and a fragrant taste. Sales are quite smooth, and even working day and night is not enough to catch up with production. This is truly a message in the voice of advocating domestic goods and saving rights.

▲Yangshupu Glen Road Xintaiyun Electric Appliance Factory declares that the factory was organized by the Hu brothers and has been in operation for five years. Electrical appliances such as electric irons, electric water pots, and electric tea kettles are designed or imitated from European goods or created by Mr. Yueshan, the owner of the factory. All of them have clever styles, are sturdy and durable, and far exceed imported products, while the prices are particularly low. Therefore, domestic and foreign electrical appliance companies are vying to purchase them first. According to this item of electrical appliances, all of them were foreign goods in the past, and Hu is the pioneer in domestic production.

Theater News 235

▲Fushang Road Baixing Grand Theater declares that the Russian revolutionary passionate war tragic giant film "Storm" recently screened at the theater is starred by John Barrymore, a famous star on the stage and in the film industry. It describes the disputes between the White and Red parties, the brutal policies of the Communist Party, and the great exposure of harassment. The intensity of the war and the passionate love are all endlessly fascinating to the audience. Therefore, despite the stormy weather in recent days, the audience at the theater is still extremely crowded.

▲YMCA declares that "A Mother's Heart" is a foreign film. The content is roughly about a wealthy woman who has fallen into decline, raising young children, marrying a daughter-in-law and having grandchildren, but her daughter-in-law is unfilial and even leaves her husband to remarry. The daughter-in-law's later experiences are full of frustration. Karma comes around, and retribution is sure. The plot is bizarre and extremely tortuous. In today's society, people are frivolous. Watching this film will surely move people and inspire them. The heart of maternal love and filial piety will arise spontaneously, and it is especially sufficient to give a shot in the arm to women who are fond of luxury and romance. The association has specially leased the film at a high price because of its relevance to morality and public sentiment. It will be screened in the auditorium of the association at 8:00 pm this Saturday. Tickets are only two cents of silver. The association's place is spacious, and the air is fresh, which is unmatched by ordinary cinemas. All those who care about social education or have a film addiction should not miss this good opportunity.

▲Jimei Film Company declares that the new film "Fearless Death" is a hilarious comedy, song, dance, and martial arts blockbuster. The plot, scenery, costumes, and photography are all the most brilliant and surpassing everything in domestic films. It is starred by Shao Zhuanglin, the "Eastern Rock". The film has now been completely completed. The company has noted that there are several scenes of great new-style song and dance in the film. It has specially discussed with the actors of the film to organize a Jimei song and dance troupe, hiring experts to guide them, and creating complete talents in the song and dance world. Since the training, several months have passed, and now they are gradually proficient, performing in a novel way, which is unmatched by other performances on stage. Various ports in South China have sent people to the company to contact them.

▲Paris Grand Theater declares that the long-rumored film "The Conflict of Soul and Flesh" has already been screened yesterday. The film is produced by Ufa Film Company, and the plot is slightly similar to "Flesh and the Devil", but the structure and expression are even more so. This is truly a rare work in modern silent films. The first show yesterday was sold out before two and a half hours had passed. The subsequent two shows were also full. The audience was very satisfied with the film.

Medical News 237

▲The second Qianchang Ginseng Store on the north side of Xiaodongmen Lane's Salted Gourd Street proclaims: reverently crafted Baibao Monkey Bezoar Powder, specializing in resolving phlegm, smoothing qi, nourishing the lungs, reducing fire, treating coughs and phlegm, and even phlegm with blood. Severe cases will be cured with three to five doses, while mild cases will be cured with one or two doses. It can also treat cold phlegm, qi-induced loss of consciousness, and seventy-two throat conditions. The price is one yuan for a large bottle and five jiao for a small bottle. They claim that it always cures illnesses.

▲Peisheng Pharmaceutical Company on Zhonghua Road proclaims: the Yijin Herb manufactured by our company specializes in treating tuberculosis and has shown considerable effectiveness. Recently, the supply of medicine has fallen short of demand, and the herbal material is about to run out. Therefore, Mr. Yang Peisheng personally took the Nanyang Maru to Hankou a few days ago and then went to Sichuan Province to collect the herb to meet the needs of patients.

▲Gong Jishetang Tuberculosis Drug Store proclaims: Physician Gong Boru is skilled in medicine and is particularly considerate of the poor and sick. Praise is often heard. Recently, he has created effective and experiential medicines for treating and preventing tuberculosis, as well as Jishetang Pills, two excellent remedies that have been proven suitable by the Central Hygiene Testing Institute. Tuberculosis medicine is specially priced at one yuan and five jiao per bottle, mainly treating new and old hemoptysis tuberculosis. Jishetang Pills are specially priced at one yuan per bottle, mainly treating acute and chronic infantile convulsions, promoting menstruation, and also treating seasonal epidemics, cholera, acute sha, and other symptoms. The general distributor is Dongqi Lane 7, Lai'an Lane, Xinmin Road, Zhabei. The distributor is Zhizhonghe Pharmacy on Sichuan Road.

▲Kyoto Tiandetang Medical Bureau proclaims: Dr. Xi Zhanyi, the director of this hall, has been practicing medicine in Shanghai for more than thirty years. His medical bureau is located opposite the Grand Theater on Sanma Road. Now, Dr. Xi has returned to Tianjin to establish the Tiande Chinese and Western General Hospital. The medical affairs of this hall are maintained by his outstanding students, Li, Xu, and Yang.

▲Jiufu Company proclaims: our company is launching a new medicine called "Buliduo" (Strength Plus). A publicity conference was held at the Great World. All advertising decorations were handled by artists and were quite ingenious, costing a considerable amount. Every evening, eyesight and memory tests were conducted, and various items were given away, also at great expense. In the past six days, more than 9,000 fans, more than 3,000 beauty pictures, more than 7,000 bottles of perfume, more than 1,000 towels, and more than 30 cosmetic boxes have been given away. Including the cost of decoration, the total cost is approximately over four or five thousand yuan. However, based on the proportion of people tested, only about one in two or three hundred people got all the answers correct. Most people could only answer about five or six correctly. This shows that the eyesight and physical strength of our people are mostly ordinary and should be quickly supplemented with Buliduo.
